22a1(14): / #/ lhan yen gyi ba ga bcas la/ legs gsol yi rang bhrul tsal gyis/ ge ba'i tshal pa mnyal 'gyur ba/ nying nas lngon par bste dang lhan/ gsung maM 'khren las yil / 
22a2(14): bayi/ drubs chen dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis/ bsrob yon badag bcas pa yi/ bar cho rkyen ngan mthar bcil nas/ bsam dag lhan gyis 'grub pa dang / mthar yang go la'i zhing khams sung / 
22a3(14): baga mthan on gnyis byang chub nas chabs cig lon n sangs rgyas par theg/ lung rtogs bstan pa'i zying po nang / sri pa'i mthar yang gnas pa ang / res me bstan 'dzin kyis ba'i / 
22a4(14): tshogs/ 'gro dan gegs med lhun grub thog/ yangs pa'i zhing khams thams cad du / nad mtshon lu ge rgyun chad nas/ 'gro rnams zhi bd ' dpal yin la/ longs su spyod pa'i bkra / 
22a5(14): shes thog/ ces pa'i 'bel dcem chen thig 'di nyid gsung dung ban gyi gnas dpal ldan khri brtan nad bo'i dtse nas slob dpen gyi ming 'dzin shangs pa bstan 'dzin 'og pas rabrag/ rnyin kbris / 
22a6(14): de phrul bo'/ zhus bgrigs shan pa'i gsal ban/ gang gsal le' chan so so'i 'ag tu gsal bshad zhus pa nad/ gong 'ag gi le' tshan rnams kyi la ds chag la/ bris pa'i chad lhag dang mngon / 
22b1(14): gal can gyi kyen m tcon rdegsl ba bkas byas pa las gang byung ges bcos thal ma byas bad ma dpo's bzhag bya te / sge bshi br lng'i dpo nin phyogs bgregs/ kyi ba grangs bad gras / 
22b2(14): bsgrigs byas yed kyang ddaung ma rtegs dbang gis chad lhag segs yod nges te/ spyi la bbayar sngen lo nga lnga brgya lhag nas gangs can bd kyi yul du yi go' pad khang 'tzugs bskun dang // pe gzhi legs / 
22b3(14): bgrigs byas pa'i 'grems yel yengs khyab byed srel dad zin na'ang / g.yung dung ben gyi dpe gzhi' bsdu bgrigs byed pa'i ga rkabs kyi hed yug de tsam byung med pas/ 'did phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len / 
22b4(14): / segs la mig nyes len gzhi dken pas gam cha gsad du yin pa dang / sges su ded zhus bsgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru / 
22b5(14): / la brling 'grig pa dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang so'i ched yug dang gnas sangs tsha las brgal ba'i legs cha zhig then thabs med pas/ de lugs kyis rjes su gzigs mtshan rnam pas 'di la dog rkyen thad ye /
